    inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1),
    0 8px 32px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);
}

  background: radial-gradient(circle at 50% 0%, #141e30 0%, #0e1320 100%);
  background-attachment: fixed;
}

/* Smooth theme transition */
html[data-theme] *,
html[data-theme] *::before,
html[data-theme] *::after {
  transition:
    background-color 0.4s ease,
    color 0.3s ease,
    border-color 0.4s ease,
    box-shadow 0.4s ease;
}
/* Exclude elements that should not animate */
html[data-theme] video,
html[data-theme] canvas,
html[data-theme] img,
html[data-theme] svg {
  transition: none;
}

/* Invert PNG icons in dark mode */
html[data-theme="dark"] .social-png-icon {
  filter: invert(1) brightness(2);
}

/* ============================================================================
 * LIQUID GLASS ANIMATIONS
 * ============================================================================
 * Animated iridescent glass effect with flowing gradient borders,
 * shimmer overlays, and refractive light shifts.
 * ============================================================================ */

@keyframes liquid-shimmer {
  0% {
    background-position: -200% center;
  }
  100% {
    background-position: 200% center;
  }
}

@keyframes liquid-border-rotate {
  0% {
    background-position: 0% 50%;
  }
  50% {
    background-position: 100% 50%;
  }
  100% {
    background-position: 0% 50%;
  }
}

@keyframes float-drift {
  0%,
  100% {
    transform: translate(0, 0) scale(1);
  }
  25% {
    transform: translate(30px, -20px) scale(1.05);
  }
  50% {
    transform: translate(-10px, 15px) scale(0.95);
  }
  75% {
    transform: translate(20px, 10px) scale(1.02);
  }
}

@keyframes pulse-glow {
  0%,
  100% {
    opacity: 0.6;
  }
  50% {
    opacity: 1;
  }
}

.liquid-glass-card {
  position: relative;
  border-radius: 30px;
  overflow: hidden;
}

  content: "";
  position: absolute;
  inset: 0;
  padding: 1.5px;
  border-radius: 30px;
  background: linear-gradient(
    120deg,
    rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.7),
    rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.7),
    rgba(56, 189, 248, 0.6),
    rgba(167, 139, 250, 0.8),
    rgba(129, 140, 248, 0.7),
    rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.7)
  );
  background-size: 400% 400%;
  animation: liquid-border-rotate 5s ease infinite;
  -webkit-mask:
    linear-gradient(#fff 0 0) content-box,
    linear-gradient(#fff 0 0);
  -webkit-mask-composite: xor;
  mask-composite: exclude;
  pointer-events: none;
}

.liquid-glass-card::after {
  content: "";
  position: absolute;
  inset: 0;
  border-radius: 30px;
  background: linear-gradient(

/**
 * ============================================================================
 * ATEION - MERGED STYLES
 * ============================================================================
 * This file contains all styles from the Ateion application.
 * ============================================================================
 */

/* ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   DESIGN TOKENS
   ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
:root {
  /* Primary Brand - Red (Ateion Brand Color) */
  --color-primary: var(--color-primary);
  --color-primary-hover: #ff5555;
  --color-primary_active: #e03e3e;
  --color-primary_light: rgba(37, 99, 235, 0.08);
  --color-primary_lighter: rgba(37, 99, 235, 0.04);

  /* Neutral Grays */
  --color-white: #ffffff;
  --color-gray-50: #fafafa;
  --color-gray-100: #f5f5f5;
  --color-gray-200: #e5e5e5;
  --color-gray-300: #d4d4d4;
  --color-gray-400: #a3a3a3;
  --color-gray-500: #737373;
  --color-gray-600: #525252;
  --color-gray-700: #404040;
  --color-gray-800: #262626;
  --color-gray-900: #171717;
  --color-black: #0a0a0a;

  /* Backgrounds */
  --color-background-primary: var(--color-background-primary);

@source '../**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}';

@import "tw-animate-css";

@layer utilities {
  @keyframes ripple {
    0% {
      transform: scale(0.5);
      opacity: 1;
    }
    100% {
      transform: scale(4);
      opacity: 0;
    }
  }

  .animate-ripple {
    animation: ripple 2.5s infinite cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  }

  .animate-ripple-delay-1 {
    animation-delay: 0.8s;
  }

  .animate-ripple-delay-2 {
    animation-delay: 1.6s;
  }
}

    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net" />
    <link
      href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Flow+Circular&family=Manrope:wght@200..800&display=swap"
      rel="stylesheet"
    />

    <!-- Anti-FOUC: Set theme before paint to prevent flash of wrong theme -->
    <script>
      (function () {
        var t = localStorage.getItem("ateion-theme");
        if (!t)
          t = window.matchMedia("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)").matches
            ? "dark"
            : "light";
        document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-theme", t);
        var m = document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]');
        if (m) m.setAttribute("content", t === "dark" ? "#0f0f11" : "#f7f3eb");
      })();
    </script>
  </head>

  <body>
    <div id="root"></div>
    <noscript>
      <div
        style="
          padding: 2rem;
          text-align: center;
          font-family: system-ui, sans-serif;
        "
      >
        <h1>Ateion — Reimagining Education</h1>
        <p>
          This application requires JavaScript to function. Please enable
          JavaScript and refresh the page.
        </p>
      </div>
    </noscript>
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
  </body>
</html>

import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import path from "path";
import tailwindcss from "@tailwindcss/vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";

export default defineConfig({
  server: {
    host: true,
    port: 3000,
    watch: {
      usePolling: true,
    },
  },
  plugins: [
    // The React and Tailwind plugins are both required for Make, even if
    // Tailwind is not being actively used – do not remove them
    react(),
    tailwindcss(),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      // Alias @ to the src directory
      "@": path.resolve(__dirname, "./src"),
      "figma:asset": path.resolve(__dirname, "./src/assets"),
    },
  },

  // File types to support raw imports. Never add .css, .tsx, or .ts files to this.
  assetsInclude: ["**/*.svg", "**/*.csv"],

  // Fix for motion-dom and lucide-react build issues
  build: {
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1600,
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          "react-vendor": ["react", "react-dom", "react-router"],
          "ui-vendor": ["framer-motion", "lucide-react", "recharts", "d3"],
          "radix-vendor": [
            "@radix-ui/react-accordion",
            "@radix-ui/react-dialog",
            "@radix-ui/react-dropdown-menu",
            "@radix-ui/react-popover",
            "@radix-ui/react-select",
          ],
        },
      },
    },
    commonjsOptions: {
      include: [/node_modules/],
    },
  },
  optimizeDeps: {
    include: ["lucide-react"],
  },
});
